<h1 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Welcome to Last War Tutorial</strong></h1>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-medium-font-size">Guides, tricks, tips and strategies for Last War: Survival Game</h2>



<blockquote class="wp-block-quote is-layout-flow wp-block-quote-is-layout-flow">
<p>Hi, I’m <strong>Cris84</strong>, and <strong>Last War Tutorial</strong> is the <strong>very first community guide website for <em>Last War: Survival Game</em></strong> and remains the <strong>most comprehensive and accurate resource available</strong>. Created even before Season 1 started, in <strong>February 2024</strong>, it has been continuously updated to cover every season since.</p>



<p>Last War Tutorial is an <strong>independent, unofficial, community-maintained website</strong>, built by players, for players. It is not operated, endorsed, or affiliated in any way with the game’s publisher.</p>



<p>Here I share <strong>my own gameplay experience</strong> and the <strong>valuable input of skilled and passionate players from the community</strong>. Everything you find on this site comes from real in-game experience.</p>



<p>Have fun, and see you in-game! 🎉</p>
</blockquote>



<p>Access the most complete and accurate Seasonal Guides:</p>

<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-medium-font-size">Disclaimer</h2>



<p><strong>Don&#8217;t trust</strong>&nbsp;guides and sites that promise unlimited diamonds/resources/power as they are all scam attempts, where they make you install a modified version of the game and then steal your phone data. Furthermore if you get noticed by the developers your account will be banned.</p>

								<a rel="nofollow" class="comment-reply-link" href="#comment-18221" data-commentid="18221" data-postid="358" data-belowelement="comment-18221" data-respondelement="respond" data-replyto="Reply to Linwei" aria-label="Reply to Linwei">Reply</a>							</div>
						</div>
					</header><!-- END .comment-header -->

					<div class="comment-meta commentmetadata">
						April 28, 2025,
						<a href="https://www.lastwartutorial.com/#comment-18221" class="comment-date">
							<time datetime="2025-04-28T02:56:15+00:00">02:56</time>
						</a>
					</div><!-- END .comment-meta -->

					<div class="comment-content">
						
						<p>Thank you for creating this Last War game guide. It has truly helped me a lot, especially in keeping up with the constantly changing gameplay.<br />
I understand that maintaining and updating such a resource alone, without sufficient support, is extremely challenging.</p>
<p>Therefore, I would like to suggest:<br />
Would you consider setting up a player submission portal, where players can contribute information,<br />
then have a small trusted group of players perform an initial review,<br />
and finally, you could consolidate and publish the refined content onto the message board?<br />
This approach could greatly reduce your workload while maintaining content quality and keeping the site alive.</p>
<p>I sincerely hope this guide can continue to exist and grow, and I believe many players are willing to support you.<br />
Regardless of your final decision, thank you very much for all the hard work and dedication you’ve put into this community. Let’s keep going!</p>
					</div><!-- END .comment-content -->

            const commentForm = document.getElementById('commentform');
            if(commentForm){
                commentForm.addEventListener('submit', function(event) {
                    var recaptchaBox = commentForm.querySelector('.g-recaptcha');                
                    if (recaptchaBox) {
                        var commentWidgetId=document.getElementById('commentform').querySelector('.g-recaptcha').getAttribute('data-widget-id');
                        var recaptchaResponse = grecaptcha.getResponse(commentWidgetId);
                        if (!recaptchaResponse) {
                            event.preventDefault();
                            // Add an error class to the reCAPTCHA box
                            recaptchaBox.classList.add('recaptcha-error');
                            alert('Please verify that you are not a robot.');
                        } else {
                            // Remove the error class if the CAPTCHA is solved
                            recaptchaBox.classList.remove('recaptcha-error');
                        }
                    }
                }, true);
            }

<script>
// Heading anchor and copy link icon
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
    // Select all heading tags h1-h6
    const headings = document.querySelectorAll("h1, h2, h3, h4, h5, h6");

    headings.forEach(heading => {
        // Only proceed if the heading has an ID and is not 'reply-title'
        if (!heading.id || heading.id === "reply-title") return;

        // Create an anchor for linking to the heading
        const anchor = document.createElement("a");
        anchor.href = "#" + heading.id;
        anchor.style.color = "inherit";
        anchor.style.textDecoration = "none";
        anchor.textContent = heading.textContent;

        // Make the heading itself a clickable link
        heading.innerHTML = "";
        heading.appendChild(anchor);

        // Create a tooltip element
        const tooltip = document.createElement("span");
        tooltip.textContent = "Click to copy link";
        tooltip.style.fontSize = "0.75em";
        tooltip.style.color = "#888";
        tooltip.style.marginLeft = "8px";
        tooltip.style.opacity = "0";
        tooltip.style.transition = "opacity 0.2s ease";
        tooltip.style.position = "absolute";
        tooltip.style.whiteSpace = "nowrap";
        tooltip.style.top = "50%"; // Center vertically
        tooltip.style.transform = "translateY(-50%)"; // Center vertically with transform

        // Position the tooltip next to the heading
        heading.style.position = "relative";
        heading.appendChild(tooltip);

        // Show tooltip on hover
        heading.addEventListener("mouseenter", function () {
            tooltip.textContent = "Click to copy link";
            tooltip.style.opacity = "1";
        });

        // Hide tooltip on mouse leave if not clicked
        heading.addEventListener("mouseleave", function () {
            if (tooltip.textContent !== "Link copied!") {
                tooltip.style.opacity = "0";
            }
        });

        // Add event listener to copy the link and change tooltip text on click
        heading.addEventListener("click", function () {
            const url = window.location.href.split("#")[0] + "#" + heading.id;
            navigator.clipboard.writeText(url).then(() => {
                tooltip.textContent = "Link copied!";
                tooltip.style.opacity = "1"; // Ensure tooltip is visible on click

                // Fade out the "Link copied!" message after 1.5 seconds
                setTimeout(() => {
                    tooltip.style.opacity = "0";
                }, 1500);
            });
        });
    });
});

</script>
<!-- END Additional Javascript Footer -->
<script>
            (function() {
                var recaptchaWidgets = [];
                var retries=0;
                var commentWidgetId = null;
                var contactUsWidgetId = null;
                var ensureRecaptchaReady = function(callback) {
                    retries++;
                    if(retries>600){
                        return;
                    }
                    if (typeof grecaptcha !== 'undefined' && typeof grecaptcha.render === 'function') {
                        callback();
                    } else {
                        setTimeout(function() { ensureRecaptchaReady(callback); }, 100);
                    }
                };
        
                var recaptchaRender = function() {
                    document.querySelectorAll('.g-recaptcha').forEach(function(widget, index) {
                        // Render only if not already rendered
                        if (!widget.hasAttribute('data-widget-id')) {
                            var widgetId = grecaptcha.render(widget);
                            widget.setAttribute('data-widget-id', widgetId);
                            recaptchaWidgets[index] = widgetId;
                        } else {
                            // Reset existing reCAPTCHA widget
                            var widgetId = widget.getAttribute('data-widget-id');
                            grecaptcha.reset(widgetId);
                        }
                    });
                };
        
                document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
                    // Lazy load reCAPTCHA when in viewport
                    var observer = new IntersectionObserver(function(entries) {
                        entries.forEach(function(entry) {
                            if (entry.isIntersecting) {
                                observer.disconnect();
                                ensureRecaptchaReady(recaptchaRender);
                            }
                        });
                    });
        
                    document.querySelectorAll('.g-recaptcha').forEach(function(widget) {
                        observer.observe(widget);
                    });
                });
        
                document.addEventListener('pageshow', function(event) {
                    if (event.persisted || performance.getEntriesByType('navigation')[0].type === 'back_forward') {
                        ensureRecaptchaReady(recaptchaRender);
                    }
                });
        
                // Fallback for older browsers without `pageshow`
                window.onpageshow = function(event) {
                    if (event.persisted) ensureRecaptchaReady(recaptchaRender);
                };
            })();
            </script>	<script>
